# The AI Ecosystem for Developers: Models, Datasets, and APIs

> AI has evolved and there is a range of people from developers, hobbyists, and tech leaders looking to explore the ecosystem. In this course, instructor Wuraola Oyewusi offers a guided exploration of the emerging AI tools developers need to know to stay competitive in their jobs. With the advent of AI tools like chat interfaces and easily accessible AI models, it can be overwhelming for those looki

### 1. Understanding the AI Ecosystem

#### What is interesting about AI?
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript

> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=0)** - What is interesting about AI?
>
> **[0:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=3)** If you're taking this course, I assume this is a question you have probably asked before, or are currently asking.
>
> **[0:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=11)** For many people, the vision of AI comes from sci-fi movies featuring robots with human-like intelligence, making decisions, and even expressing emotions.
>
> **[0:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=22)** While this is a more dramatic and entertaining depiction, the reality of AI today is both more subtle and more impactful.
>
> **[0:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=31)** AI is no longer a distant concept.
>
> **[0:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=34)** It is here, and it's shaping the world around us in ways we interact with daily.
>
> **[0:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=41)** From powering recommendation systems that suggest what to watch or buy, to enabling virtual assistant on our phones, to optimizing supply chains, predicting financial markets, analyzing your browsing habits to suggest products you might like, filter spam from your email, generating code, and even assisting in medical diagnoses, AI is behind the scenes making complex decisions in milliseconds.
>
> **[1:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=72)** The easiest way to think about AI powered systems compared to traditional software is that they leverage learning algorithms to recognize patterns from large data sets, rather than relying solely on explicit programmed roles.
>
> **[1:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=89)** So now we have AI systems that can effectively perform task once thought to be too complex, such as generating human-like text, creating realistic images, composing music, and even driving cars.
>
> **[1:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=106)** This is also fascinating because these capabilities are now very accessible, and the speed at which academic research translates into live deployment is unprecedented.
>
> **[1:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=119)** Some of the key components driving this progress are pre-trained AI models, data sets for training, and APIs that allow developers to integrate AI seamlessly.
>
> **[2:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=132)** Our goal in this course is to understand the practical components that make these systems work.
>
> **[2:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/what-is-interesting-about-ai?u=76281980&t=138)** So whether you're just curious, looking to build your own AI systems, or involved in policymaking, this course will give you a clear picture of the AI ecosystem and how to navigate it effectively.

#### Components of the AI ecosystem
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript

>
> **[0:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=11)** The closest reference is in nature.
>
> **[0:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=13)** We are living organisms interact with their environment to maintain balance and ensure survival.
>
> **[0:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=22)** Just like natural ecosystems, the AI ecosystem consists of various components that interact with and depend on each other to function effectively.
>
> **[0:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=34)** These include data, algorithms, models, frameworks, and computing infrastructure.
>
> **[0:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=43)** Each of those play a crucial role in developing and deploying AI solutions.

>
> **[0:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=57)** Data, the foundation of AI.

>
> **[1:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=69)** Whether it's images, text, speech, video, code, or sensor ratings, data serves as the foundation that powers AI models.
>
> **[1:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=82)** The quality, quantity, and diversity of data directly impacts the performance of AI solutions.
>
> **[1:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=91)** Without data, there is no learning on the (indistinct).
>
> **[1:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=96)** The data components includes data collection, gathering information from various sources such as sensors, user interactions, databases, and public repositories.
>
> **[1:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=110)** Data preparation, cleaning, organizing, and transforming raw data into useful format.
>
> **[1:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=119)** Data annotation, labeling data to provide context and meaning for supervised learning.
>
> **[2:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=127)** Data management, storing, securing, and maintaining data throughout its lifecycle.
>
> **[2:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=136)** Algorithms, the learning mechanism.
>
> **[2:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=140)** Algorithms are step by step procedures that tells computers how to process data and learn patterns.
>
> **[2:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=148)** They form the logical core of AI systems and determine our machines process information to make decisions.
>
> **[2:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=158)** Algorithms are the instructions AI models use to recognize patterns and make predictions.
>
> **[2:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=165)** Learning can be supervised.
>
> **[2:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=167)** Label built data is used to train the model or unsupervised, where the model find patterns in non labeled data.
>
> **[2:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=177)** Some key algorithms in the AI ecosystem include machine learning algorithms, linear regression, decision trees, and clustering methods.
>
> **[3:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=188)** Deep learning algorithms, these are neural networks with multiple layers for complex pattern recognition.
>
> **[3:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=197)** Reinforcement learning algorithms, these are techniques for learning through trial and errors.
>
> **[3:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=205)** Models, knowledge representation.
>
> **[3:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=210)** Models are the practical implementation of algorithms trained on specific data sets.
>
> **[3:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=216)** Once an algorithm is trained on data, it becomes an AI model.
>
> **[3:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=221)** They represent what the AI system has learned and serve as the basis for making predictions or decisions when presented with new data.
>
> **[3:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=231)** Important aspects of models include model architecture.
>
> **[3:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=236)** This is the structure and design that determines how the model processes information.
>
> **[4:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=242)** Model training, this is the process of feeding data through algorithms to create the model.
>
> **[4:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=249)** Model evaluation, testing the model's performance against validation data.
>
> **[4:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=254)** And model deployment, putting the trained model in production environment.
>
> **[4:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=261)** Frameworks, building tools.
>
> **[4:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=265)** To implement AI models efficiently, developers use frameworks.
>
> **[4:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=269)** These are software libraries and tools that simplify AI system development.
>
> **[4:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=275)** This frameworks provide previewed components and functions to implement, fine tune, and deploy AI models without starting from scratch.
>
> **[4:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=287)** Some of the most popular AI frameworks include TensorFlow, developed by Google for building and training machine learning models.
>
> **[4:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=297)** PyTorch, created by Facebook's AI research lab for flexibility and deep learning.
>
> **[5:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=304)** Scikit-learn for classical machine learning algorithms.
>
> **[5:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=309)** Hugging Face Transformers for state of the art natural language processing.
>
> **[5:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=314)** Computing infrastructure, the engine room.
>
> **[5:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=319)** Computing infrastructure provides the processing power needed to train, run, and deploy AI models.
>
> **[5:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=328)** Training and running AI models can require significant compute and power, such as graphical processing unit, GPUs, tens of processing units, TPU, and specialized AI chips that accelerate deep learning computations.
>
> **[5:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=347)** Key components of AI computing infrastructure include hardware such as GPUs, TPUs, CPUs, and specialized AI chips.
>
> **[5:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=359)** Cloud computing with services like AWS, Google Cloud, and Microsoft Azure.
>
> **[6:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=367)** Edge computing, this processes data closer to where it's generated and distributed computing using networks of computers to process large data sets.
>
> **[6:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=381)** Now that we have a grasp of some of the key components of the AI ecosystem, it's important to know that each area is vast and specialized enough to warrant its own dedicated research and career path.
>
> **[6:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/components-of-the-ai-ecosystem?u=76281980&t=395)** As we move forward, we will dive deeper into how these elements come together to power AI solutions.

#### Open-source vs. closed-source AI systems
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] By now, we have a solid foundation of the key components of the AI ecosystem, data, algorithms, models, frameworks, and computing infrastructure, and how they come together to form powerful AI systems and solutions.
>
> **[0:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=20)** But how are these solutions made available, and what are the implications of the accessibility?
>
> **[0:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=28)** Just like traditional software, AI systems can be categorized as open source or closed source, each with its own advantages, limitations, and implications for development, deployment, and ethical consideration.
>
> **[0:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=45)** It is important to distinguish between the two as we'll be exploring both open source and closed source components throughout this course.
>
> **[0:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=55)** An open source AI system is one where the code, model weights, training data or architecture are made publicly available, allowing users to study, modify, and improve upon the systems.
>
> **[1:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=72)** Some of the key features of an open source AI system are transparency and collaboration.
>
> **[1:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=79)** This means anyone can inspect, modify, and distribute the software.
>
> **[1:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=85)** Users can fine tune and modify these models to fit specific needs.
>
> **[1:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=91)** Community-driven development.
>
> **[1:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=95)** A large and active community contributes to the development and improvement of open source AI tools.
>
> **[1:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=102)** This collective effort accelerates innovation, bug fixes and feature enhancements.
>
> **[1:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=109)** Accessibility and affordability.
>
> **[1:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=112)** Open source AI systems are often free or low cost, reducing barrier to entry for individuals and organizations.
>
> **[2:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=122)** This democratizes access to AI technology, enabling smaller companies and independent developers to work with cutting edge AI.
>
> **[2:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=133)** Licensing.
>
> **[2:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=135)** Open source licenses such as the MIT license, Apache license, and GPL define the terms of use, modification and distribution.
>
> **[2:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=147)** Understanding these licenses is crucial for compliance, as they set the rules for using and modifying open source code.
>
> **[2:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=157)** A closed-source AI system is proprietary, meaning its code, model weights, or training data are not publicly available.
>
> **[2:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=167)** These models are developed by companies or research organizations, and are often monetized through API access or subscription-based service.
>
> **[2:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=178)** Proprietary technology.
>
> **[3:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=180)** Closed-source AI models and frameworks are developed and maintained by a single company or organization.
>
> **[3:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=187)** The source code is not publicly available, giving the owner exclusive control over the technology.
>
> **[3:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=194)** Commercial advantage.
>
> **[3:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=196)** Organizations often use closed-source AI to maintain a competitive edge and monetize their innovation.
>
> **[3:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=204)** This allows them to profit from research and development efforts.
>
> **[3:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=210)** Control and security.
>
> **[3:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=212)** Closed-source systems provide greater control over the technology and can offer enhanced security measures, making them suitable for sensitive applications where data privacy and reliability are critical.
>
> **[3:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=228)** Licensing.
>
> **[3:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=229)** Closed-source AI is typically licensed under proprietary terms, restricting users from modifying, distributing, or reverse engineering the software.
>
> **[4:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=241)** These licenses are often highly restrictive.
>
> **[4:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=245)** Generally, the AI ecosystem is generous, and you can achieve a lot using open source tools.
>
> **[4:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=251)** But the choice between open and closed source AI systems depends on the specific needs, priorities, and resources of the user.
>
> **[4:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=262)** If you need full control, transparency and customization, open source may be the best fit.

> **[4:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/open-vs-closed-source-ai-systems?u=76281980&t=271)** If you need reliability, security and official support, closed source could be the better option.

#### AI ethics, bias, and privacy
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=0)** - One of the biggest challenges surrounding AI adoption revolves around ethics, bias, and privacy.
>
> **[0:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=8)** As AI systems become more integrated into decision-making processes, whether in hiring, healthcare, finance, or law enforcement, questions about fairness, transparency, and data protection are relevant.
>
> **[0:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=26)** While it's tempting to prioritize immediate capabilities and dismiss those concerns, they are profoundly valid.
>
> **[0:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=35)** Ignoring them risks severe unintended consequences, including biased outcomes, privacy violations, and the critical erosion of public trust.
>
> **[0:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=48)** So, before we deep dive into the components of the AI ecosystem, it's essential that you are accurately aware of these ethical considerations.
>
> **[0:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=59)** This awareness will not only improve your approach to adopting AI tools, but also equip you with strategies to mitigate potential risks.
>
> **[1:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=70)** Ultimately, responsible AI development is not an afterthought, but a fundamental prerequisite for building trustworthy and beneficial systems.
>
> **[1:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=82)** Now, let's explore some of the key ethical concerns in AI and practical ways to address them.
>
> **[1:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=91)** Bias in datasets and models.
>
> **[1:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=93)** Concern, AI models inherent and amplify biases present in their training data, leading to unfair or discriminatory outcomes.
>
> **[1:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=107)** Some of the ways to mitigate these are, data auditing, regularly audit datasets for representation and potential biases.
>
> **[1:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=119)** Algorithmic fairness, implement fairness-aware algorithms that minimize disparities across different groups.
>
> **[2:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=129)** Diverse data collection, ensuring training data reflects the diversity of the population the AI will serve.
>
> **[2:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=140)** Privacy violations.
>
> **[2:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=142)** Concern, AI systems often collect and process vast amounts of personal data, raising risk of privacy breaches and misuse.
>
> **[2:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=154)** Some of the ways to mitigate these are, data anonymization, implement techniques to remove personally identifiable information.
>
> **[2:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=166)** Differential privacy, add controlled noise to data to protect individual privacy while preserving data utility.
>
> **[2:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=177)** Data minimization, collect only the data that is strictly necessary for the AI's intended purpose.
>
> **[3:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=187)** Strict data policies, ensure compliance with regulations like GDPR and CCPA to protect user data.
>
> **[3:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=198)** Accountability and responsibility.
>
> **[3:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=201)** The concern around this is that it can be challenging to determine who is responsible when an AI system makes a harmful or unethical decision.
>
> **[3:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=213)** Some ways to mitigate these are, clear governance, establish clear lines of responsibilities and accountability for AI development and deployment.
>
> **[3:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=225)** Ethics committees, form interdisciplinary teams to review AI projects for ethical implications.
>
> **[3:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=234)** Auditable logs, keep extensive logs of all transactions and mode versioning.
>
> **[4:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=243)** Algorithmic discrimination.
>
> **[4:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=246)** The concern around this is that AI systems can perpetuate and amplify existing social biases, leading to discriminatory outcomes in areas like lending, hiring, and criminal justice.
>
> **[4:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=263)** Some of the ways this is being mitigated is using things like fairness metrics, use metrics to assess and mitigate algorithmic discrimination.
>
> **[4:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=275)** Regular audits, conduct regular audits to identify and address discriminatory patterns.
>
> **[4:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=282)** Diverse development team, having a diverse development team helps to reduce blind spots.
>
> **[4:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=291)** Misinformation and manipulation.
>
> **[4:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=295)** AI-powered tools can be used to generate highly realistic fake images, videos, and texts, which are then used for misinformation to manipulate public opinion and undermine democratic processes.
>
> **[5:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=312)** Some of the ways to mitigate these are, media literacy, promote media literacy to help people critically evaluate information.
>
> **[5:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=322)** Fact checking tools, develop and deploy AI-powered fact checking tools.
>
> **[5:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=329)** And in some instances, watermarking, who have developed systems to watermark AI-generated content.
>
> **[5:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=338)** Lack of transparency, black box AI.
>
> **[5:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=342)** Many AI systems lack transparency, making it difficult to understand how they reach their decision.
>
> **[5:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=350)** This reduces accountability and trust.
>
> **[5:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=354)** Some of the ways to undo these are encouraging explainable AI, develop models that provide interpretable explanations of their decisions.
>
> **[6:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=366)** Model documentation, maintain detailed records of AI decision-making processes and training data sources.
>
> **[6:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=375)** Regulatory compliance, follow emerging AI transparency laws and ethical guidelines.
>
> **[6:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=383)** Automation and job displacement.
>
> **[6:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-ethics-bias-and-privacy?u=76281980&t=387)** This is a popular concern around AI adoption, and the concern is that AI-driven automation can replace human jobs, increasing unemployment and widening economic inequality.
>

### 2. AI Models and Architecture

#### Introduction to AI models and architecture
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980)

> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=0)** - If your exposure to software systems is not from an AI-related background, you might find discussions about AI models and architectures lacking context.
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=12)** AI models and architectures are influential in determining the capabilities, performance, and scalability of AI systems.
>
> **[0:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=23)** An AI model is a learned representation of data patterns, enabling systems to make predictions, generate insights, or automate tasks.
>
> **[0:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=35)** It processes input data and generates outputs that reflect the system's understanding or decision-making process.
>
> **[0:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=46)** These models are created using large amounts of data, which the system uses to identify patterns and relationships.
>
> **[0:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=55)** For example, if you're using an AI assistant like a chatbot or voice assistant, the model powering it is a large language model capable of generating human-like text responses and understanding complex queries.
>
> **[1:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=72)** Architecture, on the other hand, is the structural design of the AI system.
>
> **[1:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=77)** It encompasses how models are built, connected, and optimized for specific tasks.
>
> **[1:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=85)** Architecture defines how various components, such as models, data pipelines, processing units, and algorithms interact and work together to achieve desired outcomes.
>
> **[1:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=101)** The architecture is essential in ensuring that the system runs efficiently and can scale to meet the demand of complex tasks.
>
> **[1:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=111)** For example, the large language model powering the AI assistant is based on the Transformer architecture or a variant, which allows it to process and understand long sequences of text efficiently.
>
> **[2:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=126)** There are many ways to classify AI model architectures.
>
> **[2:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=130)** By data processing approach, an AI architecture can be unimodal, which focuses on processing a single type of data, for example, text, image, or audio.
>
> **[2:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=145)** On the other hand, multimodal architectures process and integrate multiple types of data.
>
> **[2:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=153)** These models can combine text, images, audio, and even video input to perform more sophisticated tasks.
>
> **[2:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=164)** By primary function, AI model architecture can be generative, where they create new content, or predictive, where they forecast or classify existing data.
>
> **[2:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=178)** Generative architectures produce outputs that resemble the input data, while predictive models focus on extracting insights from it.
>
> **[3:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=189)** By origin, they may also be a base or foundational architecture or a variant or a fine-tuned model built upon them.
>
> **[3:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=200)** Base architectures provide the core framework, while variants are customized for specific use cases or improved performance.
>
> **[3:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=210)** By domain specialization: Natural Language Processing, or NLP, architectures are designed for processing and understanding sequential data like text and speech.
>
> **[3:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=223)** Computer vision architectures are designed for processing and interpreting images and videos.
>
> **[3:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=231)** The typical AI architecture components are: input processing layers that prepare raw data for the model.
>
> **[4:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=241)** Feature extraction mechanisms to identify patterns in input.
>
> **[4:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=248)** Computational units that perform calculations and transformation.
>
> **[4:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=254)** And then the output generation layer to produce results.
>
> **[4:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=260)** Some of the key considerations in architectural design and choices are computational efficiency to minimize resource consumption, scalability to ensure they can do increasing complexity, task-specific optimization, and generalization.
>
> **[4:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-models-and-architecture?u=76281980&t=281)** This is the capability to ensure the model can perform well among synced data.
>

#### NLP architectures: RNNs and transformers
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Natural language processing, NLP, is the subfield of AI focused on sequences like text and speech.
>
> **[0:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=10)** AI architecture in this domain are designed to model sequential dependencies, making them essential for tasks like language modeling, translation, and text generation.
>
> **[0:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=25)** Some of the most popular model architecture used in NLP include recurrent neural networks, RNNs.
>
> **[0:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=33)** RNNs are a class of neural networks designed for sequential data, where previous inputs influence future predictions.
>
> **[0:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=43)** The components of RNNs include the input layer, which processes sequences like words or full names.
>
> **[0:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=52)** Hidden state stores memory of previous inputs, allowing the model to retain context.
>
> **[0:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=59)** Output layer produces predictions such as the next word in a sentence.
>
> **[1:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=66)** Recurrent connections connects the hidden layer to itself, allowing information to persist across time steps.
>
> **[1:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=76)** RNNs are used for language modeling, predicting the next word in a sequence, machine translation, translating text from one language to another, speech recognition, converting spoken language into text, sentiment analysis, determining the emotional tone of a text, time series analysis, predicting future values based on past observation.
>
> **[1:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=106)** RNNs were introduced in the 1980s, but gained popularity in the 2010s with applications in speech recognition and machine translation.
>
> **[1:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=118)** However, the struggle with long-range dependencies due to issues like vanishing gradients.
>
> **[2:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=125)** This led to the development of more advanced variants, such long short-term memory, LSTM.
>
> **[2:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=134)** LSTM is designed to capture long-term dependencies using gating mechanisms.
>
> **[2:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=140)** LSTMs include memory cells and gates that control the flow of information.
>
> **[2:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=147)** Gated recurrent unit, GRUs.
>
> **[2:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=151)** This is a simplified version of LSTMs with fewer parameters, making it more computationally efficient.
>
> **[2:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=160)** Transformers.
>
> **[2:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=162)** Transformers are a class of neural network architectures that has revolutionized NLP by replacing sequential processing with parallelized self-attention mechanism.
>
> **[2:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=175)** Unlike RNNs, which process data step by step, transformers can analyze entire sequences at once, making them more efficient and effective for large-scale NLP application.
>
> **[3:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=189)** Components of transformers include input embeddings.
>
> **[3:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=194)** This converts words or subwords into dense vector representation.
>
> **[3:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=201)** Positional encoding.
>
> **[3:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=202)** This adds information about word order since transformers process all tokens in parallel.
>
> **[3:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=210)** Self-attention mechanism.
>
> **[3:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=213)** This determines the importance of different words in a sentence relative to each other.
>
> **[3:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=219)** Feedforward layer further transform representations after attention mechanism.
>
> **[3:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=226)** Layer normalization and dropout.
>
> **[3:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=229)** This improves stability and prevents overfeeding.
>
> **[3:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=233)** Output layer.
>
> **[3:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=235)** This generates predictions based on land representations.
>
> **[4:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=240)** Some use cases of transformers are text generation, used in models like GPT for producing human-like text, machine translation, powering translation tools like Google Translate, sentiment analysis, identifying emotions in text-based data, question answering, enabling AI assistants to understand and respond to queries, text summarization, condensing long documents into concise summaries.
>
> **[4:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=274)** Transformers were introduced in 2017 with the paper, "Attention Is All You Need" by Vaswani and others.
>
> **[4:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=283)** The breakthrough was eliminating the sequential nature of RNNs, allowing for better scalability and parallel processing.
>
> **[4:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=293)** This led to the development of various transformer-based models such as BERT, Bidirectional Encoder Representations from Transformers.
>
> **[5:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=304)** This is trying to understand context, input direction, making it highly effective for comprehension-based tasks.
>
> **[5:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=313)** GPT, Generative Pre-trained Transformer, focuses on text generation used in applications like Chat-GPT.
>
> **[5:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=322)** T5, text-to-text transfer transformer, converts all NLP tasks into a unified text-to-text format.
>
> **[5:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=333)** XLNet, an extension of BERT with improved autoregressive modeling capability.
>
> **[5:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/natural-language-processing-architectures-rnns-and-transformers?u=76281980&t=340)** Apart from the architectures mentioned here, there are many other architectures for sequences that are worth studying.

#### Computer vision architectures: CNNs and vision transformers

>

>

>

>

>

#### Generative architectures: Diffusion and GANs
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Generative AI architecture focus on creating new data instances that resemble the training data.
>
> **[0:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=8)** They can generate images, text, and even audio data resembling real-world examples.
>
> **[0:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=16)** They are useful for tasks such as image sentences, text generation, and audio creation.
>
> **[0:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=25)** Two permanent generative architectures are diffusion models and generative adversarial networks, GANs.
>
> **[0:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=35)** Diffusion models are a class of generative models that operate on the principle of gradually adding noise to an image and then learning to reverse this process to generate new data.
>
> **[0:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=49)** It is inspired by how diffusion works in physics, where particles spread out from high to low concentration.
>
> **[0:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=57)** In diffusion models, the goal is to learn how to reverse this diffusion process, transforming random noise into structured data.
>
> **[1:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=68)** The key components of a diffusion model include forward process, where you gradually add noise to the input data until it becomes pure noise.
>
> **[1:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=80)** Reverse process, the model learns to reverse the noise addition, gradually recovering the original image from noisy data.
>
> **[1:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=90)** Predictor, this predicts the noise added at each step of the forward process, enabling the reverse process.
>
> **[1:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=100)** And then sampling, this generates new data by starting with noise and applying the reverse diffusion process.
>
> **[1:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=109)** There are many uses for diffusion models, including image generation, where you can create high quality images from text description or random noise image.
>
> **[2:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=122)** Image resolution, modifying existing images by denoising them to improve their quality.
>
> **[2:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=131)** Video generation, generating realistic video sequences from textural description.
>
> **[2:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=139)** Diffusion models gained prominence in recent years due to their ability to generate high-fidelity images and their stability during training.
>
> **[2:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=150)** This led to the development of various diffusion model variants, such as DDPM, Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Models, a foundational diffusion model that uses a fixed variant schedule for diffusion process.
>
> **[2:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=168)** Stable Diffusion, a latent diffusion model that operates in lower dimensional latent space, improving efficiency.
>
> **[2:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=179)** Imageen, a text to image diffusion model that achieves high levels of photorealism and text alignment.
>
> **[3:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=188)** Generative adversarial networks, GANs, are designed to generate realistic data by training two neural networks, the generator and the discriminator, in competition with each other.
>
> **[3:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=203)** These networks are trained simultaneously, where the generator learns to create fake data, and the discriminator learns to distinguish between real and generated data.
>
> **[3:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=215)** The goal is for the generator to create data so realistic that the discriminator cannot tell the difference.
>
> **[3:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=224)** Some components of GAN include generator.
>
> **[3:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=229)** This is the model responsible for generating synthetic data.
>
> **[3:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=233)** It learns to create data that mimic real world data distribution.
>
> **[3:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=238)** Discriminator.
>
> **[4:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=240)** This is the model responsible for distinguishing between real and synthetic data samples.
>
> **[4:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=246)** It acts as a judge of the data authenticity.
>
> **[4:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=250)** Adversarial training.
>
> **[4:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=252)** The generator tries to fool the discriminator while the discriminator tries to correctly identify real samples.
>
> **[4:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=260)** Loss functions.
>
> **[4:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=262)** This guides the training process, encouraging the generator to produce realistic samples and the discriminator to actively classify samples.
>
> **[4:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=274)** Some uses of GAN include image synthesis, where it generates realistic images from random noise or specific inputs, such as faces, objects, and landscapes.
>
> **[4:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=289)** Style transfer, applying the style of one image to another.
>
> **[4:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=294)** Image super-resolution, increasing the resolution of low-resolution images.
>
> **[5:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=301)** And data augmentation, generating synthetic data to augment training dataset.
>
> **[5:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=308)** GANs were first introduced in 2014 by Ian Goodfellow and others in the paper, "Generative Adversarial Networks."
>
> **[5:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=319)** The innovation was the adversarial training process, which enabled the generation of highly realistic data.
>
> **[5:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=328)** This led to the development of various GAN variants, such as DCGAN, Deep Convolutional GAN.
>
> **[5:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=336)** This uses convolutional neural networks for both the generator and discriminator.
>
> **[5:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=342)** StyleGAN, this generates high-resolution photorealistic images with fine-grained control over style.
>
> **[5:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=352)** CycleGAN performs on paired image to image translation.
>
> **[5:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/generative-architectures-diffusion-and-gans?u=76281980&t=357)** These architectures are interesting because they are used for real-world task across industries, not just research, from fashion and creative fields to medical industry.

#### Multimodal architectures: CLIP and Flamingo
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/multimodal-architectures-clip-and-flamingo?u=76281980)

>
> **[0:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/multimodal-architectures-clip-and-flamingo?u=76281980&t=16)** These architectures are contemporary, so they are very recent, as recent as the 2020s.

>
> **[0:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/multimodal-architectures-clip-and-flamingo?u=76281980&t=32)** CLIP is a neural network that learns to connect visual and texture representations.
>

>
> **[2:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/multimodal-architectures-clip-and-flamingo?u=76281980&t=121)** Text-based image editing, modifying images based on textual instructions.

>

>

>

>

>
