#### Efficient architectures
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Efficient AI architectures focus on optimizing computational performance, reducing model size, and improving inference speed while maintaining high accuracy.
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=12)** These architectures are designed to make AI models more practical for deployment, on resource-constraint devices like edge devices, mobile application, and large scale cloud environments.
>
> **[0:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=28)** They are designed to optimize the trade-off between model performance and computational resources.
>
> **[0:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=35)** Some of the most popular efficient AI architectures include MobileNet.
>
> **[0:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=41)** MobileNets are lightweight convolutional neural networks designed for efficient image processing on mobile and edge devices.
>
> **[0:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=51)** They achieve high accuracy while significantly reducing computational cost, making them suitable for real life application.
>
> **[1:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=61)** Some of the components of MobileNet include depth-wise convolution.
>
> **[1:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=66)** This applies a single filter to each input channel, reducing the number of parameters by factoring standard convolution into depth-wise.
>
> **[1:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=77)** Point-wise convolution.
>
> **[1:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=79)** This combines the output of depth-wise convolution using one by one convolutions.
>
> **[1:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=86)** Width multipliers.
>
> **[1:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=88)** This allows for controlling the models width and computational complexity.
>
> **[1:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=94)** It adjusts the number of filters per layer to trade off between accuracy and efficiency.
>
> **[1:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=101)** Resolution multiplier.
>
> **[1:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=104)** This allows for controlling the input resolution and computational complexity.
>
> **[1:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=109)** It scales the input image resolution to balance accuracy and computational cost.
>
> **[1:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=116)** Global average pooling.
>
> **[1:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=118)** This reduces the number of parameters in fully connected layers while preserving essential features.
>
> **[2:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=127)** Some of the uses of MobileNet include mobile vision applications for image classification, object detection, and segmentation on mobile devices.
>
> **[2:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=138)** Embedded systems, vision task on devices with limited computational resources.
>
> **[2:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=145)** Real-time applications, applications requiring fast inference speed.
>
> **[2:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=151)** Robotics, vision task on robots with limited onboard processing.
>
> **[2:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=157)** Augmented reality and virtual reality.
>
> **[2:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=161)** MobileNet enables AI-powered AR filters and object tracking.
>
> **[2:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=167)** MobileNet was introduced in 2017 by Andrew G.
>
> **[2:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=171)** and others from Google in the paper "MobileNets: Efficient Convolutional Neural Networks for Mobile Vision Applications."
>
> **[3:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=181)** Its key innovation was using depth-wise separable convolution to reduce computational cost.
>
> **[3:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=189)** This led to the development of various MobileNet versions such as MobileNetV2, which introduces inverted residuals and linear bottlenecks to improve accuracy and efficiency.
>
> **[3:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=204)** MobileNetV3, which incorporates neural architecture search and hard-swish activation to further optimize performance.
>
> **[3:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=214)** EfficientNet.
>
> **[3:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=216)** EfficientNet is a family of CNN architectures designed to achieve state-of-the art performance while using significantly fewer parameters and FLOPs.
>
> **[3:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=227)** FLOPs mean floating-point operations per second.
>
> **[3:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=232)** It introduces a novel scaling method to optimize network depth, width, and resolution.
>
> **[4:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=240)** Some of the components of EfficientNet include compound scaling.
>
> **[4:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=245)** This scales the network dimensions using compound coefficient.
>
> **[4:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=250)** It balances depth, width, and resolution to improve efficiency.
>
> **[4:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=256)** Squeeze-and-excitation blocks.
>
> **[4:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=259)** This enhances future representation by modeling channel wise dependencies.
>
> **[4:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=265)** Swish activation function.
>
> **[4:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=268)** This provides smooth gradient flow for better optimization.
>
> **[4:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=272)** MBConv blocks.
>
> **[4:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=274)** This uses mobile inverted bottleneck convolution blocks.
>
> **[4:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=280)** Some of the use cases for EfficientNet include image classification.
>
> **[4:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=285)** It achieves high accuracy with fewer parameters.
>
> **[4:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=288)** It outperforms large models while using fewer resources.
>
> **[4:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=294)** Object detection, efficient object detection on various platforms in real time.
>
> **[5:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=300)** Edge computing, deploying efficient models on edge devices like smart camera.
>
> **[5:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=307)** EfficientNet was introduced in 2019 by Mingxing and others from Google in the paper "Rethinking Model Scaling for Convolutional Neural Networks."
>
> **[5:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=320)** Its key innovation was the compound scaling method.
>
> **[5:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=324)** This led to the development of various EfficientNet versions such as EfficientNetV2, which improves training speed and parameter efficiency.
>
> **[5:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=336)** DistilBERT.
>
> **[5:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=338)** DistilBERT is a compressed version of BERT transformer model, designed to retain most of its capabilities while reducing its size and improving speed.
>
> **[5:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=349)** It achieves efficiency through knowledge distillation where a smaller student model learns from a larger teacher model.
>
> **[5:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=359)** Components of DistilBERT include fewer transformer layers.
>
> **[6:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=364)** It uses six layers instead of BERT 12 reducing computational cost.
>
> **[6:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=370)** Knowledge distillation.
>
> **[6:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=372)** It trains the model using soft labels from a pretrained BERT model.
>
> **[6:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=378)** Weight sharing, reduces redundant parameters for greater efficiency.
>
> **[6:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=385)** Dynamic token pruning, speeds up inference by skipping unnecessary computation.
>
> **[6:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=392)** Some use cases for BERT include question answering, used in AI chatbot and virtual assistant.
>
> **[6:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=399)** Text summarization, efficiently condenses long document.
>
> **[6:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=404)** Sentiment analysis such as analyzing customer reviews and social media data.
>
> **[6:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=410)** And natural language understanding, where it powers lightweight NLP applications.
>
> **[6:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=419)** DistilBERT was introduced in 2019 by Hugging Face and it reduces the computational requirement of transformers while preserving up to 97% of BERT's performance.
>
> **[7:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/efficient-architectures?u=76281980&t=434)** Understanding the availability of efficient AI models and architectures is important because typical AI models are large and deployment on smaller devices is a valid and almost inevitable use case, as you progress in your career.

>
> **[0:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-datasets?u=76281980&t=45)** A dataset is a structured collection of data that is used to train, validate, and test AI models.
>
> **[0:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-datasets?u=76281980&t=53)** It can contain images, text, audio, numerical values, or a combination of multiple data types, depending on the AI application.

> **[1:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-datasets?u=76281980&t=65)** It is used to train, validate, and test machine learning models.
>
> **[1:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-datasets?u=76281980&t=69)** It typically consists of a set of samples where each sample contains features, and in supervised learning, corresponding labels or targets.
>
> **[1:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-datasets?u=76281980&t=80)** Essentially, a data set transforms raw, unstructured information into a format that AI models can understand and learn from.
>
> **[1:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/introduction-to-ai-datasets?u=76281980&t=91)** Raw data refers to unprocessed data, while datasets has raw data that has been cleaned, organized, and formatted for use in machine learning models.
>

#### Foundational AI image datasets

> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] There has been a lot of interesting work done with images in AI.

> **[0:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=16)** Foundational datasets are datasets that serve as the basis for training, evaluating, and benchmarking AI models.
>
> **[0:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=26)** They are well established, widely used in research, and often designed to cover fundamental tasks.
>
> **[0:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=34)** The key characteristics of foundational datasets are broad applicability.
>
> **[0:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=40)** They are used across multiple AI applications and research areas.
>
> **[0:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=46)** They are well documented and created.
>
> **[0:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=49)** Often created with standardized labeling and annotation.
>
> **[0:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=54)** They are used as benchmarking standards.
>
> **[0:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=56)** That means they serve as reference point to compare model performance.
>
> **[1:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=63)** They're publicly available, typically freely accessible for researchers and developers to experiment with, and many of them have historical significance.
>
> **[1:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=74)** That means they have played a key role in advancing AI techniques.
>
> **[1:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=80)** Some of the foundational image datasets used in AI are MNIST.
>
> **[1:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=85)** Modified National Institute of Standards and Technology.
>
> **[1:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=90)** The MNIST dataset introduced by Yann LeCun, Corinna Cortes and Christopher Burges in 1998 is one of the most well-known dataset in computer vision.
>
> **[1:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=102)** It was derived from the original NIST and written digital dataset.
>
> **[1:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=108)** MNIST contains 60,000 training images and 10,000 test images of unwritten digits with each image in 28 x 28 in grayscale and it has labels represent digits from zero to nine, making 10 classes.
>
> **[2:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=129)** Some of its use cases are benchmarking image classification models, testing convolutional neural networks, CNNs for digital recognition, developing handwritten digital recognition system for OCR systems, and serving as an introductory dataset for deep learning and computer vision research.
>
> **[2:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=153)** CIFAR, Canadian Institute of Advanced Research.
>
> **[2:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=157)** The CIFAR datasets developed by Canadian Institute of Advanced Research and the University of Toronto were introduced by Alex Vino and Geoffrey Hinton in 2009 to benchmark image classification models.
>
> **[2:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=176)** These datasets were derived from the larger datasets called Tiny Images created at MIT.
>
> **[3:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=184)** There is CIFAR-10 containing 60,000 color images, 32 x 32 pixel across 10 categories such as airplanes, cars, and trucks.
>
> **[3:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=198)** Each category has 6,000 images and with 50,000 for training and 10,000 for testing and 700, which is more complex with a hundred categories instead of 10.
>
> **[3:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=214)** Each category has 600 images making classification more challenging.
>
> **[3:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=220)** Some of the use cases include benchmarking image classification models in deep learning research.
>
> **[3:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=226)** Early state deep learning experiments, especially for CNN development and testing new architectures before scaling to larger dataset.
>
> **[3:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=237)** ImageNet, the ImageNet dataset introduced by Fei-Fei Li and her team at Stanford University in 2009.
>
> **[4:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=245)** It was designed to create the large scale visual database for AI models, significantly advancing computer vision.
>
> **[4:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=254)** The main dataset contains over 40 million labeled images across more than 21,000 categories.
>
> **[4:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=262)** Then there is the ImageNet Large Scale Visual Recognition Challenge, ILSVRC, containing 1000 categories with 1.2 training images, 50,000 validation images, and 100,000 test images.
>
> **[4:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=282)** Some of its use cases are training deep CNNs for large-scale image classification, benchmarking image recognition models.
>
> **[4:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=291)** For example, AlexNet, VGG, ResNet and EfficientNet.
>
> **[4:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=297)** Object detection and localization tasks and transfer learning where pre-trained ImageNet models are fine tuned for other computer vision tasks.
>
> **[5:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=309)** Pascal VOC.
>
> **[5:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=311)** Pattern analysis, statistical modeling and computational learning visual object classes.
>
> **[5:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=318)** The Pascal VOC developed as part of the Pascal Visual Object Classes challenge was introduced in 2005.
>
> **[5:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=327)** It includes over 20 categories such as person, car, dog, and bicycle.
>
> **[5:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=335)** It is used for training object detection model, such as faster R-CNN and YOLO.
>
> **[5:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=342)** Semantic segmentation task and evaluating model generation on real-world objects.
>
> **[5:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=349)** COCO.
>
> **[5:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=350)** Common objects in context.
>
> **[5:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=353)** The COCO dataset developed by Microsoft introduced in 2014 was designed to improve AI models' ability to understand objects in real world context, including detailed annotation for object bounding boxes, segmentation mask and image captions.
>
> **[6:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=374)** It contains over 330,000 images with over 200,000 labeled images in 80 categories.
>
> **[6:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=385)** It also features 1.5 million object instances.
>
> **[6:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=390)** COCO use cases include object detection using models like faster R-CNN, YOLO, and RetinaNet.
>
> **[6:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=398)** Instance segmentation for example, Mask R-CNN for pixel-level object detection.
>
> **[6:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=405)** Image captioning, where AI generates descriptive text for images.
>
> **[6:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=412)** Action recognition and scene understanding for autonomous systems.
>
> **[6:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=417)** Open Images.
>
> **[6:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=419)** Open Images launched by Google in 2016 is a large scale dataset designed for object detection, segmentation, and visual relationship detection.
>
> **[7:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=431)** It has over 9 million images with 36 million annotations in about 19,000 categories.
>
> **[7:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=440)** Its use cases include large scale object detection and recognition, scene understanding in real world images, visual relationship detection, where AI models understand object interaction and weakly supervised learning, where models learn from large scale noisy dataset.
>
> **[7:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=461)** We have explored only a fraction of the image dataset available for AI.
>
> **[7:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=467)** There are domain specific dataset such as TextPad and x-ray dataset for medical imaging.
>
> **[7:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-image-datasets?u=76281980&t=473)** It is worth exploring more of these for your understanding and hopefully for integration into your workflow.

#### Foundational AI text datasets
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] The shared volume and availability of unstructured data, such as text, is one of the key factors why the AI ecosystem has progressed rapidly in recent times.
>
> **[0:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=13)** Foundational text datasets are essential resources that provide the textual data necessary for training, evaluating, and benchmarking natural language processing, NLP models.
>
> **[0:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=27)** They are characterized by their broad applicability, well-documented structure, and historical significance in advancing NLP techniques.
>
> **[0:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=39)** Many of the foundational AI text datasets have their root and origin in linguistics and information retrieval, and text data used in NLP are often referred to as corpus, plural, corpora.
>
> **[0:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=55)** A corpus is a large and structural set of text, typically used for linguistic analysis, statistical processing, and AI model training.
>
> **[1:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=66)** Some of the most widely used foundational text datasets include the Brown Corpus.
>
> **[1:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=72)** Compiled at Brown University in the 1960s, this is one of the earliest electronic corpora of American English.
>
> **[1:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=80)** It contains approximately 1 million words of text from various sources, including news articles, fiction, and nonfiction.
>
> **[1:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=92)** Its uses include linguistic analysis and research, training early statistical NLP models, and developing part-of-speech tagging and parsing algorithms.
>
> **[1:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=107)** Penn Treebank, PTB.
>
> **[1:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=110)** Introduced in the early '90s by the University of Pennsylvania, this is one of the earliest and most widely used linguistic datasets.
>
> **[1:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=119)** It contains syntactically parsed text from sources such as "The Wall Street Journal."
>
> **[2:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=126)** Some of its uses include part-of-speech tagging, syntactic parsing for linguistic analysis, language modeling benchmarks.
>
> **[2:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=137)** Reuters-21578.
>
> **[2:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=141)** The Reuters-21578 dataset is a collection of news articles from the Reuters newswire, categorized into various topics.
>
> **[2:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=151)** It was also introduced in the 1990s, and contains thousands of documents, making it a standard benchmark for text classification.
>
> **[2:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=161)** Some of its use cases include text classification and categorization, information retrieval and topic modeling, and evaluating the performance of machine learning algorithms on text data.
>
> **[2:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=175)** Wikipedia dumps.
>
> **[2:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=177)** Wikipedia provides freely available text dumps of its articles, making it one of the most extensive resources for natural language understanding.
>
> **[3:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=187)** It covers from 2001 to present.
>
> **[3:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=191)** It is commonly used for tasks like large-scale language modeling and pre-training, for example, in training BERT and and GPT, named entity recognition and knowledge extraction, and summarization and question-answering tasks.
>
> **[3:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=210)** Common Crawl.
>
> **[3:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=212)** Common Crawl is a massive dataset consisting of petabytes of web-crawled data, providing raw text from websites across the internet in different languages.
>
> **[3:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=224)** It's been crawled since 2008 till now.
>
> **[3:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=228)** It is used in large-scale unsupervised learning and web-based knowledge extraction and text mining.
>
> **[3:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=238)** SQuAD, Stanford Question Answering Dataset.
>
> **[4:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=242)** SQuAD, developed at Stanford in 2016, is a large-scale question-answering dataset containing passages from Wikipedia with corresponding questions and human-annotated answers.
>
> **[4:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=256)** It's used for training and benchmarking QA models, fine-tuning transformer models like BERT and T5, and information retrieval for AI-powered search systems.
>
> **[4:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=269)** GLUE, General Language Understanding Evaluation benchmark.
>
> **[4:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=273)** The GLUE dataset was introduced in 2018 as a benchmark to evaluate general NLP model performance across multiple tasks such as sentiment analysis, textual entailment, and question answering.
>
> **[4:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=290)** Its use cases include benchmarking NLP models, evaluating general language understanding, and training models for diverse NLP tasks.
>
> **[5:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=302)** Just as with image dataset, we have only explored a fraction of the text datasets available for AI.
>
> **[5:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundational-ai-text-datasets?u=76281980&t=310)** There are many domain-specific datasets, such as PubMed for medical text analysis.

#### Foundational AI speech datasets
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript

> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Processing speech data has always been a significant task in computation.
>
> **[0:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=5)** As with other data types, advancement in AI has been significantly driven by the availability of large and high-quality speech datasets.
>
> **[0:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=16)** This dataset enabled the training and evaluation of models for tasks like speech recognition, speaker identification, and audio analysis.
>
> **[0:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=27)** In this video, we would explore some of the foundational AI speech datasets that has been instrumental in this progress.
>
> **[0:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=36)** Not every speech dataset meets all this criteria, but some key characteristics of foundational speech datasets include size and diversity, covering a wide range of speakers, accents and recording condition, high quality annotation, providing accurate transcriptions and speaker labels, standardized formats, ensuring compatibility across different models and tools, public availability, facilitating open research and development, and also, historical significance, contributing to the evolution of speech processing techniques.
>
> **[1:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=79)** Some of the most widely used foundational speech datasets include TIMIT Acoustic-Phonetic Continuous Speech Corpus, developed by Texas Instrument, MIT and SRI International in the 1980s.
>
> **[1:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=95)** It is one of the first phonetically-transcribed speech dataset.
>
> **[1:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=99)** It contains 630 speakers, reading phonetically balanced sentences.
>
> **[1:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=107)** Some of its use cases are acoustic-phonetic modeling, phoneme recognition and speech segmentation, training and evaluating speech recognition systems, and studying speaker and dialect variations.
>
> **[2:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=123)** LibriSpeech.

> **[2:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=125)** Released in 2015, librispeech is derived from audiobook recording of LibriVox, containing around 1,000 hours of English speech.
>
> **[2:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=137)** The dataset provides clean and noisy speech samples, along with the aligned transcript.
>
> **[2:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=145)** Its use cases include benchmarking deep-learning automatic speech recognition models, pre-training transformer-based speech models like wav2vec and Whisper.
>
> **[2:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/foundation-ai-speech-datasets?u=76281980&t=156)** Speaker diarization and speaker verification task.

> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/explore-librispeech-dataset?u=76281980&t=12)** Torchaudio is a library built on top of PyTorch that provides tools for loading, processing, and analyzing audio data efficiently.

> **[0:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/explore-librispeech-dataset?u=76281980&t=22)** It includes datasets, transformations, and pre-trained models for speech-related task.

>
> **[0:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-development-tools-and-frameworks-debugging-and-versioning?u=76281980&t=3)** So beyond choosing the right languages, ideas, and frameworks, building reliable and reproducible AI systems heavily relies on two crucial practices, rigorous debugging and meticulous versioning.
>
> **[0:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-development-tools-and-frameworks-debugging-and-versioning?u=76281980&t=19)** While these are essential in all software development, let's explore the specific tools and techniques that are particularly useful for AI development.
>
> **[0:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-development-tools-and-frameworks-debugging-and-versioning?u=76281980&t=30)** Some of the challenges related to debugging AI and machine learning systems include data problems.
>
> **[0:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-development-tools-and-frameworks-debugging-and-versioning?u=76281980&t=37)** Errors can arise from poor quality data, hidden biases, incorrect labels, or shift between training and real-world data distribution.
>
> **[0:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-development-tools-and-frameworks-debugging-and-versioning?u=76281980&t=47)** Debugging often involve intensive data exploration and validation.
>
> **[0:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-development-tools-and-frameworks-debugging-and-versioning?u=76281980&t=53)** Model Behavior.
>
> **[0:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-development-tools-and-frameworks-debugging-and-versioning?u=76281980&t=55)** Models might fail to convert during training, suffer from exploding or vanishing gradients, leading into non-values.
>
> **[1:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-development-tools-and-frameworks-debugging-and-versioning?u=76281980&t=64)** Exhibit unexpected predictions or show poor generalization.
>
> **[1:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-development-tools-and-frameworks-debugging-and-versioning?u=76281980&t=70)** Understanding why a model behaves a certain way can be challenging.
>
> **[1:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-development-tools-and-frameworks-debugging-and-versioning?u=76281980&t=75)** Performance issues.
>
> **[1:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-development-tools-and-frameworks-debugging-and-versioning?u=76281980&t=77)** Identifying bottlenecks related to data loading, GPU utilization, memory leaks, or inefficient computations is critical, especially when working with large data sets and complex models.
>

#### AI computing infrastructure
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] If your interaction has been with basic software systems, you probably don't think much about the computing infrastructure.
>
> **[0:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=7)** However, training complex AI models involves billions of parameters and processing massive data sets which demand substantial computational power.
>
> **[0:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=18)** In fact, one of the key reasons AI has become practical and scalable in recent years is the evolution of computing infrastructure that can efficiently handle the mathematical operations required for machine learning.
>
> **[0:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=33)** AI models, especially deep learning models, require immense computational resources to handle the complex mathematical operations involved in tasks like training neural networks.
>
> **[0:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=47)** Specialized hardware accelerators such as GPUs, graphical processing units, or TPUs, tensor processing units, are specifically designed to accelerate these operations, making it possible to train models faster and more efficiently than traditional CPUs.
>
> **[1:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=66)** Other evolving accelerators are NPUs, neural processing units, integrated into CPUs; or SoCs, system-on-chip; FPGAs, field-programmable gate arrays; and custom ASICs designed for specific AI task, particularly efficient inference on the edge.
>
> **[1:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=89)** Training some AI models can take days or weeks even on high-end GPU clusters, making access to robust infrastructure a critical success factor.
>
> **[1:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=101)** In addition to training inference at scale, such as having predictions to millions of users, also requires optimized compute resources.
>
> **[1:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=110)** To meet those demands, there are three approaches to infrastructure: cloud-based, on-premise, and hybrid.
>
> **[1:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=119)** The choice between them depend on factors like project scale, budget, privacy, and long-term needs.
>
> **[2:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=127)** Cloud.
>
> **[2:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=129)** Cloud providers like Amazon Web Services, Google Cloud, and Microsoft Azure offer on-demand access to powerful computing resources specifically optimized for AI workload.
>
> **[2:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=143)** Cloud-based infrastructure offers flexibility, scalability, and no maintenance overload.
>
> **[2:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=149)** It is particularly well-suited for startups, research teams, or organizations that requires temporary burst of computing power or want to experiment and prototype without large upfront investment.
>
> **[2:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=165)** The ability to dynamically scale resources makes these a great option for handling variable workload, running large-scale experiments, or deploying models globally.
>
> **[2:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=179)** Many cloud platforms also offer pre-configured machine learning environment, reducing set up time, and simplifying the training to deployment pipeline.
>
> **[3:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=190)** While cloud options typically involved lower initial cost, organizations should carefully evaluate the long-term cost of ownership as ongoing subscription fees can exceed on-premise cost for stable high-utilization workload.
>
> **[3:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=207)** On-premise means that organizations purchase, install, operate, and maintain its own dedicated AI computing hardware.
>
> **[3:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=215)** These are servers equipped with GPUs, accelerators, the storage and networking within its own data centers or facilities.
>
> **[3:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=226)** This approach offers maximum control over the infrastructure, data security and configuration.
>
> **[3:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=232)** While it requires significant upfront capital investment and dedicated IT expertise for management and upkeep, it can be more cost effective for constant, high-utilization workloads or when strict data sovereignty regulations apply.
>
> **[4:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=250)** It also allows for fine-grain hardware customization, including selection of specific GPU models, memory configuration, and interconnect tailored to AI workloads.
>
> **[4:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=261)** On-premise setup can offer lower latency and greater data throughput for sensitive use cases like real-time video processing or autonomous systems.
>
> **[4:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=271)** Organizations with specialized performance requirements often benefit from on-premise setups where they can optimize the entire hardware stack for their specific care application.
>
> **[4:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=284)** Hybrid infrastructure combines both cloud and on-premise resources, allowing organizations to take advantage of the flexibility of the cloud while maintaining control and security over a certain workload on premise.
>
> **[5:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=300)** This balanced approach provides a best-of-both-worlds solution that addresses different aspects of AI development lifecycle.
>
> **[5:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=309)** This approach is particularly useful for companies that want to keep sensitive data in house, but still need the elastic scalability of cloud resources for tasks like large-scale model training or sieving.
>
> **[5:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=322)** For example, training could be done in the cloud using massive GPU clusters while inferences handled on premise to meet latency or privacy requirement.
>
> **[5:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=335)** Hybrid models offer a balanced approach, enabling businesses to optimize for cost, performance, and compliance simultaneously.
>
> **[5:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=345)** They are ideal for organization undergoing digital transformation or scaling from local R-and-D environment to production-grade systems.
>
> **[5:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=355)** Hybrid architectures also facilitate smoother migration paths, allowing organizations to gradually transition workloads between environment as their needs evolve.
>
> **[6:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=369)** As AI models grow in complexity and scale, the choice of computing infrastructure becomes a strategic decision.
>
> **[6:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=377)** Whether leveraging the cloud for its flexibility, deploying on-premise for control and compliance, or adopting an hybrid approach for the best of both worlds, aligning your infrastructure with your project goal is essential to delivering scalable, high-performing and sustainable AI solutions.
>
> **[6:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-computing-infrastructure?u=76281980&t=398)** The right infrastructure decision should balance immediate technical needs with long-term business objectives, considering not just the performance and cost, but also factors like team expertise, data governance requirements, and anticipated growth pattern.

#### AI model rankings: Leaderboards, benchmarks, and evaluation trends
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] In AI, performance isn't just discussed, it's measured.
>
> **[0:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=4)** Unlike traditional software engineering where success can often be defined in binary terms, for example, it works or it doesn't, AI model performance is nuanced and deeply context dependent.
>
> **[0:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=21)** Evaluating models reliably requires clearly defined task, standardized data sets, reproducible matrix, and a shared understanding of what better actually means.
>
> **[0:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=34)** This is where model ranking, benchmarking, and leaderboards come into play.
>
> **[0:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=40)** They provide standardized ways to assess the capabilities of models across various tasks and datasets, helping researchers, practitioners, and businesses make informed decision.
>
> **[0:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=56)** The field is continuously evolving with new benchmarks and evaluation methodologies.
>
> **[1:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=61)** Imagine to address the increasing complexity and capability of AI models.
>
> **[1:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=68)** Benchmarks and leaderboards are based on metrics, and metrics are quantitative measures used to evaluate the performance of AI models on specific task and dataset.
>
> **[1:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=80)** So to lay a good foundation for our discussion, let's explore some of the most common performance metrics, used in AI.
>
> **[1:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=90)** Accuracy, the proportion of correct predictions; precision, the accuracy of positive predictions; recall, the ability of the model to identify all relevant instances; F1 score, the harmonic precision and recall; BLEU, bilingual evaluation understudy; and ROUGE, recall-oriented understudy for gisting evaluation for evaluating the quality of generated text in natural language processing tasks.
>
> **[2:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=126)** Mean absolute error, MAE, and mean squared error, MSE.
>
> **[2:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=132)** For regression task, measuring the difference between predicted and actual values.
>
> **[2:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=138)** Area under the ROC curve, AUC-ROC, for binary classification.
>
> **[2:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=145)** Evaluating the model's ability to distinguish between classes.
>
> **[2:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=150)** Tool selection quality, TSQ, a matrix used to assess how well AI agents utilize tools for giving tasks.
>
> **[2:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=161)** Benchmarks typically consist of standardized datasets paired with evaluation metrics for specific tasks, such as image classification, object detection, language modeling, or summarization.
>
> **[2:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=175)** They provide a consistent framework to assess and compare the performance of AI models.
>
> **[3:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=183)** Popular benchmarks include ImageNet, a large dataset of labeled images used for image classification tasks, GLUE, general language understanding evaluation, and SuperGLUE, benchmarks for evaluating the performance of natural language understanding models across a variety of tasks.
>
> **[3:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=206)** SQuAD, Stanford question answering dataset, a reading comprehension benchmark.
>
> **[3:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=213)** ARC, abstraction and reasoning corpus, a benchmark for testing advanced reasoning in AI models.
>
> **[3:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-model-rankings-leaderboards-benchmarks-and-evaluation-trends?u=76281980&t=222)** Humanity's last exam, HLE, a challenging benchmark across multiple domains to evaluate the overall capability of AI models.
>

#### AI interoperability standards: Model Context Protocol (MCP)
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-interoperability-standards-model-context-protocol-mcp?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-interoperability-standards-model-context-protocol-mcp?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Just as traditional software systems benefit from shared protocols and standards, AI systems now require the same foundation.
>
> **[0:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-interoperability-standards-model-context-protocol-mcp?u=76281980&t=8)** It is becoming increasingly essential for AI systems to achieve seamless interoperability.
>
> **[0:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-interoperability-standards-model-context-protocol-mcp?u=76281980&t=16)** As the ecosystem of AI tools, agents, and models grow more complex, this ability to pass information cleanly, consistently, and contextually between components is key to building robust scalable AI applications, and that's where model context protocol, MCP, comes in.
>
> **[0:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-interoperability-standards-model-context-protocol-mcp?u=76281980&t=40)** MCP is an emerging standard designed to enable interoperability across AI tools, frameworks, and models.
>
> **[0:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-interoperability-standards-model-context-protocol-mcp?u=76281980&t=49)** At its core, MCP defines a structured schema for serializing context.
>

>
> **[1:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/ai-interoperability-standards-model-context-protocol-mcp?u=76281980&t=69)** Think of it as a common language or contract that tools and models can use to talk to each other.

### Conclusion

#### Summary
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/the-ai-ecosystem-for-developers-models-datasets-and-apis/conclusion?u=76281980)
